<table>
<table>

<tr>

</th>

<dl><dd>I. [no tempo marking]
</dd><dd>II. Largo
</dd><dd>III. Presto
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year

<td>1738
</td></tr>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Concertos&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Concertos</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_harpsichord%2C_strings%2C_continuo&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For harpsichord, strings, continuo</a></span>;
